add_namespace = pacificstates
add_namespace = KX_california
add_namespace = calpeaceout

### 1937 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # Commonwealth Nomination
	id = pacificstates.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.1"}
	title = pacificstates.1.t
	desc = pacificstates.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Upton Sinclair
		name = pacificstates.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_commonwealth_primary_sinclair
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.6
				days = 35
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Culbert Olson
		name = pacificstates.1.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_commonwealth_primary_olson
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.6
				days = 35
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1937 Dem-Rep Primary
	id = pacificstates.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.3"}
	title = pacificstates.3.t
	desc = pacificstates.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Earl Warren
		name = pacificstates.3.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_warren
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 6
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # William Gibbs McAdoo
		name = pacificstates.3.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_mccadoo
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 6
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Clarence D. Martin
		name = pacificstates.3.c
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_martin
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 6
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Charles A. Sprague
		name = pacificstates.3.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_sprague
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Manchester Boddy
		name = pacificstates.3.f
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_boddy
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep Landon
		name = pacificstates.3.g
		trigger = {
		has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Alf Landon" }
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = 0.03
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_landon
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2
				days = 6
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1937 Republican Primary
	id = pacificstates.4
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.4"}
	title = pacificstates.4.t
	desc = pacificstates.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Robert Taft
		name = pacificstates.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_taft
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Harry Chandler
		name = pacificstates.4.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_government = market_liberal
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_gellatly
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Howard Hughes
		name = pacificstates.4.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_hughes
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Frank Merriam
		name = pacificstates.4.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_merriam
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Frank Knox
		name = pacificstates.4.f
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_knox
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Louis B. Meyer
		name = pacificstates.4.g
		trigger = {
		has_country_flag = CAL_immigrant_presidents
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_meyer
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep Curtis
		name = pacificstates.4.h
		trigger = {
		has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Charles Curtis" }
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = 0.03
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_curtis
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.3
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1937 Democrat Primary
	id = pacificstates.5
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.5"}
	title = pacificstates.5.t
	desc = pacificstates.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Henry J. Kaiser
		name = pacificstates.5.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_kaiser
		}
			country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.4
			days = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2080
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Charles Martin
		name = pacificstates.5.b
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_martin
		}
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.4
			days = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2080
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Walt Disney
		name = pacificstates.5.c
		add_political_power = -10
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_disney
		}
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.251
			days = 2
		}
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.4
			days = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2080
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Keep Garner
		name = pacificstates.5.e
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "John Nance Garner" }
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		add_stability = 0.03
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_garner
		}
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.4
			days = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2080
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # John McGroarty
		name = pacificstates.5.f
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_mcgroarty
		}
		country_event = {
			id = pacificstates.4
			days = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.2080
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1937 Election
	id = pacificstates.6
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.6"
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
		}
	}
	title = pacificstates.6.t
	desc = pacificstates.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		has_elected_government = yes
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PSA_had_1937_election
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_election_occured
			if = { # Upton Sinclair
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_commonwealth_primary_sinclair
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Upton Sinclair"
					desc = "POLITICS_UPTON_SINCLAIR_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Upton_Sinclair.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
					traits = { author }
				}
			}
			if = { # Culbert Olson
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_commonwealth_primary_olson
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Culbert Olson"
					desc = "POLITICS_CULBERT_OLSON_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Culbert_Olson.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
					traits = { silent_workhorse }
				}
			}
			if = { # Henry Wallace
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_wallace
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Henry Wallace"
					desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_WALLACE_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_Henry_Wallace.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = { great_survivor }
				}
			}
			if = { # Charles McNary
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_mcnary
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Charles McNary"
					desc = "POLITICS_CHARLES_MCNARY_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_Charles_L_McNary.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = { fortification_engineer }
				}
			}
			if = { # Hiram Johnson
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_johnson
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Hiram Johnson"
					desc = "POLITICS_HIRAM_JOHNSON_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Hiram_Johnson.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = { captain_of_industry }
				}
			}
			if = { # C.C. Young
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_progressive_primary_young
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "C.C. Young"
					desc = "POLITICS_CC_YOUNG_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/CAL_CC_Young.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = { diehard_progressive }
				}
			}
			if = { # Earl Warren
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_warren
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Earl Warren"
					desc = "POLITICS_EARL_WARREN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Earl_Warren.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = { backroom_backstabber }
				}
			}
			if = { # William Gibbs McAdoo
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_mccadoo
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "William Gibbs McAdoo"
					desc = "POLITICS_WILLIAM_GIBBS_MCADOO_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/CAL_William_Gibbs_Mcaddo.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = { eco_bank_president }
				}
			}
			if = { # Clarence D. Martin
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_martin
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Clarence D. Martin"
					desc = "POLITICS_CLARENCE_MARTIN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Clarence_Martin.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = { fortification_engineer }
				}
			}
			if = { # Charles A. Sprague
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_sprague
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Charles A. Sprague"
					desc = "POLITICS_CHARLES_SPRAGUE_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Charles_A_Sprague.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = { economic_reformer }
				}
			}
			if = { # Manchester Boddy
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_liberal_primary_boddy
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Manchester Boddy"
					desc = "POLITICS_MANCHESTOR_BODDY_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/CAL_Manchester_Boddy.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = { editor }
				}
			}
			if = { # Robert Taft
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_taft
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Robert Taft"
					desc = "POLITICS_Robert_Taft_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/CAL_R_A_Taft.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = { staunch_constitutionalist }
				}
			}
			
			if = { # Harry Chandler
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_chandler
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Harry Chandler"
					desc = "POLITICS_HARRY_CHANDLER_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/CAL_HarryChandler.png.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = { eco_industrialiser }
				}
			}

			if = { # Howard Hughes
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_hughes
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Howard Hughes"
					desc = "POLITICS_HOWARD_HUGES_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/CAL_Howard Hughes.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = { captain_of_industry }
				}
			}
			
			if = { # Frank Merriam
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_merriam
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Frank Merriam"
					desc = "POLITICS_FRANK_MERRIAM_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Frank_Merrimam.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = { prince_of_terror }
				}
			}
			if = { # Frank Knox
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_knox
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Frank Knox"
					desc = "POLITICS_FRANK_KNOX_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Frank_Knox.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = { sec_media_magnate }
				}
			}
			if = { # Louis B Meyer
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_republican_primary_meyer
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Louis B. Meyer"
					desc = "POLITICS_LOUIS_B_MEYER_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/CAL_Louis_B._Mayer.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = { sec_media_magnate }
				}
			}
			if = { # Charles Martin
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_martin
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Charles Martin"
					desc = "POLITICS_CHARLES_MARTIN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/CAL_Charles_Henry_Martin.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = { hog_reformist_soldier }
				}
			}
			if = { # Henry J. Kaiser
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_kaiser
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Henry J. Kaiser"
					desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_J_KAISER_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/CAL_Henry_J_kaiser.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = { eco_industrialiser }
				}
			}
			if = { # Walt Disney
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_disney
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Walt Disney"
					desc = "POLITICS_WALT_DISNEY_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/CAL_Walt_Disney.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = { propaganda_expert }
				}
			}
			if = { # John McGroarty
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1937_democratic_primary_mcgroarty
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "John S. McGroarty"
					desc = "POLITICS_JOHN_MCGROARTY_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/CAL_John_McGroarty.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = { sec_media_magnate }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Progressive
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAL_political
						option = CAL_POLITICAL_PATH_COMMONWEALTH
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAL_political
						option = CAL_POLITICAL_PATH_DEMREP
					}					
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAL_political
						option = CAL_POLITICAL_PATH_REPUBLICAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAL_political
						option = CAL_POLITICAL_PATH_DEMOCRAT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAL_political
						option = CAL_POLITICAL_PATH_HEARST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAL_political
						option = CAL_POLITICAL_PATH_BODIN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAL_political
						option = CAL_POLITICAL_PATH_JAPAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAL_political
						option = CAL_POLITICAL_PATH_AISO
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAL_political
						option = CAL_POLITICAL_PATH_DISNEY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAL_political
						option = CAL_POLITICAL_PATH_HUGHES
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CAL_political
						option = CAL_POLITICAL_PATH_NORTON
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = pacificstates.6.a
		set_country_flag = PSA_had_1937_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1937_election_progressive
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = CAL_Henry_Wallace_hog_sde
			add_ideas = CAL_Ralph_Johnson_Bunche_for_sde
			add_ideas = CAL_Hjalmar_Petersen_eco_sde
			add_ideas = CAL_Konrad_Knute_Solberg_sec_sde

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.7
				days = 1276
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.10
				days = 1297
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.6000
				days = 380
			}

country_event = { # Democratic-Republicans Join the Progressives
	id = pacificstates.6000
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.6000"}
	title = pacificstates.6000.t
	desc = pacificstates.6000.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
	tag = CAL
	NOT = {
		has_country_flag = CAL_dem_rep_system
		}
	}

	option = { # Good
		name = pacificstates.6000.a
		add_political_power = 45
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = -0.06 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		set_country_flag = CAL_dem_rep_system
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			long_name = CAL_prog_dominance_long
			name = CAL_prog_dominance_party }	
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_Progs_Win
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.6006
				days = 35
			}
		}
	}
}

			name = CAL_radical_dominance_party }	
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_Radicals_Win
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.6010
				days = 35
			}
		}
	}
}

### 1940 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1940 Progressive Primary
	id = pacificstates.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.7"}
	title = pacificstates.7.t
	desc = { # Progressive won in 1940
		text = pacificstates.7.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive won in 1940
		text = pacificstates.7.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = PSA_Progs_Win
		tag = CAL
		has_elected_government = yes	
		date > 1940.1.1
		date < 1945.1.1	
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PSA_had_1940_election
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
	days = 1
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Homer Bone
		name = pacificstates.7.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_bone
		}
	}
	option = { # Sheridan Downey
		name = pacificstates.7.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_downey
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep the President
		name = pacificstates.7.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
	option = { # Oswald West
		name = pacificstates.7.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_west
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1940 Democrat Primary
	id = pacificstates.1000
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.1000"}
	title = pacificstates.1000.t
	desc = pacificstates.1000.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress
	
	immediate = {
	set_country_flag = Dem_survive
	}
	
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = PSA_Conservatives_Win
		NOT = {
		OR = {
			has_government = paternal_autocrat
			has_government = national_populist
			has_government = syndicalist
			has_government = totalist
			}
		}
		tag = CAL
		has_elected_government = yes
		date > 1940.1.1
		date < 1945.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PSA_had_1940_election
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Keep the Presidency
		name = pacificstates.1000.a
		trigger = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.02 }
	}
	option = { # Upton Sinclair
		name = pacificstates.1000.b
		trigger = {
		NOT = {
		has_country_leader = {
				name = "Upton Sinclair"
				ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1940_commonwealth_primary_sinclair
		}
	}
	option = { # Culbert Olson
		name = pacificstates.1000.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Culbert Olson"
				ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {

		}
	}

country_event = { # 1940 election
	id = pacificstates.11
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.11"
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
		}
	}
	title = pacificstates.11.t
	desc = pacificstates.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		has_democratic_government = yes
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PSA_had_1940_election
		}
		date > 1940.1.1
		date < 1945.1.1
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1940_commonwealth_primary_sinclair
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Upton Sinclair"
					desc = "POLITICS_UPTON_SINCLAIR_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Upton_Sinclair.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
					traits = { author }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1940_commonwealth_primary_olson
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Culbert Olson"
					desc = "POLITICS_CULBERT_OLSON_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CAL/Portrait_CAL_Culbert_Olson.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
					traits = { silent_workhorse }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_wallace
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Henry Wallace"
					desc = "POLITICS_HENRY_WALLLACE_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Henry_Wallace.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = { great_survivor }
				}
			}
			if = { # Homer Bone
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_bone
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Homer Bone"
					desc = "POLITICS_HOMER_BONE_DESC"
					picture = "CAL_Homer_Bone.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = { backroom_backstabber }
				}
			}
			if = { # Sheridan Downey

				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Sheridan Downey"

					picture = "CAL_sheridan_downey.png"

					traits = { silent_workhorse }
				}
			}
			if = { # Earl Warren
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1940_liberal_primary_warren
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Earl Warren"
					desc = "POLITICS_EARL_WARREN_DESC"

	option = { # Progressive
		name = pacificstates.11.a
		trigger = {
		has_country_flag = PSA_Progs_Win
		}
		set_country_flag = PSA_had_1940_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1940_election_progressive
			if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_democrat }
			set_country_flag = CAL_social_democrats_win_twice_flag
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1940_progressive_primary_wallace
				}
				add_ideas = CAL_Henry_Wallace_hog_sde
				add_ideas = CAL_Ralph_Johnson_Bunche_for_sde
				add_ideas = CAL_Hjalmar_Petersen_eco_sde
				add_ideas = CAL_Konrad_Knute_Solberg_sec_sde
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_leader = {
						name = "Huey Long"
						ruling_only = yes
						}
						has_idea = CAL_Huey_Long_hog_sde
					}
				}
				add_ideas = CAL_Huey_Long_hog_sde
				add_ideas = CAL_Ralph_Johnson_Bunche_for_sde
				add_ideas = CAL_Hjalmar_Petersen_eco_sde
				add_ideas = CAL_Konrad_Knute_Solberg_sec_sde
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = CAL_Henry_Wallace_hog_sde
				add_ideas = CAL_Ralph_Johnson_Bunche_for_sde
				add_ideas = CAL_Hjalmar_Petersen_eco_sde
				add_ideas = CAL_Konrad_Knute_Solberg_sec_sde
			}

			# next primaries
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.12
				days = 1276
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.13
				days = 1283
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.14
				days = 1290
			}
			country_event = {
				id = pacificstates.15
				days = 1297
			}
		}
	}

### 1944 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1944 Progressive Primary
	id = pacificstates.12
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.12"}
	title = pacificstates.12.t
	desc = { # Progressive Party won the presidency just last time
		text = pacificstates.12.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = PSA_1940_election_progressive
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party won also in 1940
		text = pacificstates.12.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = PSA_1940_election_progressive
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency
		text = pacificstates.12.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		has_country_flag = PSA_Progs_Win
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = PSA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = PSA_had_1940_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PSA_had_1944_election
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Glen H. Taylor
		name = pacificstates.12.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
				has_country_flag = PSA_1940_election_progressive
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1944_progressive_primary_taylor
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep the Presidency
		name = pacificstates.12.c
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = PSA_1940_election_progressive
			}
		}
	}
}

	option = { # President is re-elected
		name = pacificstates.15.e
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = PSA_1940_election_democrat
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1944 election
	id = pacificstates.16
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.16"
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
		}
	}
	title = pacificstates.16.t
	desc = pacificstates.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = PSA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = PSA_had_1944_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PSA_had_1944_election
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Glen H. Taylor
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1944_progressive_primary_taylor
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Glen H. Taylor"
					desc = "POLITICS_GLEN_TAYLOR_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Glen_Taylor.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					traits = { figurehead_president }
				}
			}
			if = { # Monrad Wallgren
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1944_progressive_primary_wallgren
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Monrad Wallgren"
					desc = "POLITICS_MONRAD_WALLGREN_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Monrad_Charles_Wallgren.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = { silent_workhorse }
				}
			}
			if = { # Clyde Tingley
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1944_progressive_primary_tingley

				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Clyde Tingley"
					desc = "POLITICS_CLYDE_TINGLEY_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Clyde_Tingley.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_liberal_subtype
					traits = { fortification_engineer }
				}
			}
			if = { # Arthur B. Langlie
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1944_republican_primary_langlie
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Arthur B. Langlie"
					desc = "POLITICS_ARTHUR_LANGLIE_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Arthur_B_Langlie.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"

					traits = { financial_expert }
				}
			}
			if = { # Douglas McKay
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1944_republican_primary_mckay
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Douglas McKay"
					desc = "POLITICS_DOUGLAS_MCKAY_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Douglas_McKay.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = { captain_of_industry }
				}
			}
			if = { # Fletcher Bowron
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1944_republican_primary_mckay
					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Fletcher Bowron"
					desc = "POLITICS_FLETCHER_BOWRON_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Fletcher_Bowron.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = market_liberal_subtype
					traits = { nationalist_symbol }
				}
			}

				limit = {

					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }

				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Daniel I. J. Thornton"
					desc = "POLITICS_DANIEL_THORNTON_DESC"

					NOT = { has_country_flag = CAL_Norton_PSA_flag }
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Bourke B. Hickenlooper"
					desc = "POLITICS_BOURKE_HICKENLOOPER_DESC"
					picture = "Portrait_CAL_Bourke_B_Hickenlooper.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					traits = { reluctant_interventionist }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Progressive
		name = pacificstates.16.a
		trigger = {
		has_country_flag = PSA_Progs_Win
		}
		set_country_flag = PSA_had_1944_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1944_election_progressive

			elections_allowed = yes

				limit = {

### 1948 Elections and Primaries ###
country_event = { # 1948 Progressive Primary
	id = pacificstates.17
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.17"}
	title = pacificstates.17.t
	desc = { # Progressive Party won the presidency just last time
		text = pacificstates.17.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = PSA_1944_election_progressive
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = PSA_1944_election_progressive
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party won also in 1944
		text = pacificstates.17.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = PSA_1944_election_progressive
			has_country_flag = PSA_1944_election_progressive
		}
	}
	desc = { # Progressive Party does not have the Presidency
		text = pacificstates.17.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		has_elected_government = yes
		has_country_flag = PSA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = PSA_had_1944_election
		has_country_flag = PSA_had_1944_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PSA_had_1948_election
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Glen H. Taylor
		name = pacificstates.17.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
				AND = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_country_flag = PSA_1944_election_progressive
					has_country_flag = PSA_1944_election_progressive
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PSA_1948_progressive_primary_taylor
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep the Presidency
		name = pacificstates.17.c
		Trigger = {
			AND = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				has_country_flag = PSA_1944_election_progressive
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PSA_1944_election_progressive
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {

### Foreign Policy 22 - 49###
country_event = { # America is reunited
	id = pacificstates.22
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.22"}
	title = pacificstates.22.t
	desc = pacificstates.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = CAL
		NOT = {
			country_exists = TEX
			country_exists = CSA
			country_exists = USA
			country_exists = COR
		}
		owns_state = 361 #Maryland
		owns_state = 371 #Louisiana
		owns_state = 395 #Illinois
		owns_state = 797 #San Francisco
		owns_state = 932 #Massachusetts
		has_war = no		
	}

	option = { # at long last we are reunited
		name = pacificstates.22.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = CAl_peaceoutgang
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = PSA_reunited_america_flag
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = PSA_Norton_america } }
			set_cosmetic_tag = NEE_america
			else = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = CAL_Norton_PSA
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			remove_ACW_cores = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # at long last we are reunited
		name = pacificstates.22.b
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAl_peaceoutgang
		}
		country_event = calpeaceout.11
		every_state = {
			remove_ACW_cores = yes
		}
	}
}

### Domestic Policy Events 50 - 75 ###
country_event = { # Formation of HUAC
	id = pacificstates.50
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event pacificstates.50"}
	title = pacificstates.50.t
	desc = pacificstates.50.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
		tag = CAL
		tag = USA
		}
		OR = {
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_over_flag
		has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_avoided_flag
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_government = social_liberal
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 6
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_completed_focus = CAL_red_scare
		}
	}

	option = { # HUAC is Formed
		name = pacificstates.50.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		add_stability = -0.1
	}
	option = { # HUAC is not Formed
		name = pacificstates.50.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_conservative
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

		has_completed_focus = CAL_trial_of_american_companies
	}

	}

			}

				id = pacificstates.68
				days = 14
			}

				id = pacificstates.69
				days = 21

				id = pacificstates.70
				days = 28
			}
		}
	}

			factor = 40
		}
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
		set_country_flag = USA_weapon_companies_allowed

	}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}

	}

			add_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
		limit = {
		has_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_4_left
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_4_left
			add_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
		limit = {
		has_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_4_right
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_4_right
			add_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_5
			}
		}
		else_if = {
		limit = {
		has_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_4_both
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_4_both
			add_idea = CAL_Marshall_plan_idea_5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {# I like it how it is
		name = pacificstates.203.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
	}
}

			}
		set_country_flag = PSA_1937_election_occured

			limit = { has_global_flag = USA_civil_war_begun_flag }
			CAL = { declare_war_on = { target = WCC type = annex_everything	} }

				NOT = {
					has_war_with = COR
				}
			}
			CAL = { declare_war_on = { target = COR type = annex_everything	} }

				NOT = {
					has_war_with = CSA
				}
			}
			CAL = { declare_war_on = { target = CSA type = annex_everything	} }
		}

			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = TEX
				}
			}
			CAL = { declare_war_on = { target = TEX type = annex_everything	} }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claimed_by = USA

		}
	}
